                     +'<img src="/img/ajax-loader.gif" />'; 
                     +'</div>';
     var mehr_lesen = '<div class="m-t-4 styling-to-top" id="bottom">'

                     +'  <a href="javascript:void(0);" data-currPage="1"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-load-more"><i class="icon icon-arrow-circle-down"></i><br class="visible-xs-block" />Weitere Nachrichten</button></a>'

                     + '</div>';
     
     var $ajax_button    = $("div.ajax-container-button:last");
     var $ajax_container = $("div.ajax-container-items:last");
     
     
     function mkLazy() {
         $("img.lazy").lazy({
              effect: "fadeIn",
              effectTime: 200,
              bind: "event",
              // css-Klasse "lazy" entfernen nach dem Laden
              afterLoad: function(element) {
                  element.removeClass("lazy");
              }
         });
     }
     
     
     
   $(document).ready(function () {
       $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
  
       if( history.state != null) {
         $ajax_container.html(history.state.ajax_content);
         $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
         mkLazy();
       };
     
       $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
         scroll(0,0);
       });
 
       $('.SiteHeaderSticky_close').hide();
   });
  if( history.state != null) {
     var more_news_currPage = history.state.more_news_currPage;
  } else {
      var more_news_currPage = 1;
  }
  var more_news_maxPerPage = 10;
     
  $( ".ajax-container-button" ).on( "click", function() {
      $( this ).html(loading_gif );
    
      $.ajax({
         url: "news/ajax",
         data: { 
             currPage : more_news_currPage, 
             maxperpage : more_news_maxPerPage
         },
         error: function(xhr){
             $ajax_container.append('Leider können derzeit keine weiteren News geladen werden.');
         }, 
         success: function(result){
             more_news_currPage ++;
             $ajax_container.hide().append(result).fadeIn(300);
             $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
             $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
             mkLazy();
             history.pushState( {ajax_content: $ajax_container.html() , more_news_currPage: more_news_currPage }, '', '#bottom');
             $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
               scroll(0,0);
             });
         }
       });

                     +'<img src="/img/ajax-loader.gif" />'; 
                     +'</div>';
     var mehr_lesen = '<div class="m-t-4 styling-to-top" id="bottom">'

                     +'  <a href="javascript:void(0);" data-currPage="1"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-load-more"><i class="icon icon-arrow-circle-down"></i><br class="visible-xs-block" />Weitere Nachrichten</button></a>'

                     + '</div>';
     
     var $ajax_button    = $("div.ajax-container-button:last");
     var $ajax_container = $("div.ajax-container-items:last");
     
     
     function mkLazy() {
         $("img.lazy").lazy({
              effect: "fadeIn",
              effectTime: 200,
              bind: "event",
              // css-Klasse "lazy" entfernen nach dem Laden
              afterLoad: function(element) {
                  element.removeClass("lazy");
              }
         });
     }
     
     
     
   $(document).ready(function () {
       $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
  
       if( history.state != null) {
         $ajax_container.html(history.state.ajax_content);
         $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
         mkLazy();
       };
     
       $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
         scroll(0,0);
       });
 
       $('.SiteHeaderSticky_close').hide();
   });
  if( history.state != null) {
     var more_news_currPage = history.state.more_news_currPage;
  } else {
      var more_news_currPage = 1;
  }
  var more_news_maxPerPage = 10;
     
  $( ".ajax-container-button" ).on( "click", function() {
      $( this ).html(loading_gif );
    
      $.ajax({
         url: "news/ajax",
         data: { 
             currPage : more_news_currPage, 
             maxperpage : more_news_maxPerPage
         },
         error: function(xhr){
             $ajax_container.append('Leider können derzeit keine weiteren News geladen werden.');
         }, 
         success: function(result){
             more_news_currPage ++;
             $ajax_container.hide().append(result).fadeIn(300);
             $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
             $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
             mkLazy();
             history.pushState( {ajax_content: $ajax_container.html() , more_news_currPage: more_news_currPage }, '', '#bottom');
             $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
               scroll(0,0);
             });
         }
       });

                     +'<img src="/img/ajax-loader.gif" />'; 
                     +'</div>';
     var mehr_lesen = '<div class="m-t-4 styling-to-top" id="bottom">'

                     +'  <a href="javascript:void(0);" data-currPage="1"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-load-more"><i class="icon icon-arrow-circle-down"></i><br class="visible-xs-block" />Weitere Nachrichten</button></a>'

                     + '</div>';
     
     var $ajax_button    = $("div.ajax-container-button:last");
     var $ajax_container = $("div.ajax-container-items:last");
     
     
     function mkLazy() {
         $("img.lazy").lazy({
              effect: "fadeIn",
              effectTime: 200,
              bind: "event",
              // css-Klasse "lazy" entfernen nach dem Laden
              afterLoad: function(element) {
                  element.removeClass("lazy");
              }
         });
     }
     
     
     
   $(document).ready(function () {
       $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
  
       if( history.state != null) {
         $ajax_container.html(history.state.ajax_content);
         $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
         mkLazy();
       };
     
       $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
         scroll(0,0);
       });
 
       $('.SiteHeaderSticky_close').hide();
   });
  if( history.state != null) {
     var more_news_currPage = history.state.more_news_currPage;
  } else {
      var more_news_currPage = 1;
  }
  var more_news_maxPerPage = 10;
     
  $( ".ajax-container-button" ).on( "click", function() {
      $( this ).html(loading_gif );
    
      $.ajax({
         url: "news/ajax",
         data: { 
             currPage : more_news_currPage, 
             maxperpage : more_news_maxPerPage
         },
         error: function(xhr){
             $ajax_container.append('Leider können derzeit keine weiteren News geladen werden.');
         }, 
         success: function(result){
             more_news_currPage ++;
             $ajax_container.hide().append(result).fadeIn(300);
             $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
             $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
             mkLazy();
             history.pushState( {ajax_content: $ajax_container.html() , more_news_currPage: more_news_currPage }, '', '#bottom');
             $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
               scroll(0,0);
             });
         }
       });

                     +'<img src="/img/ajax-loader.gif" />'; 
                     +'</div>';
     var mehr_lesen = '<div class="m-t-4 styling-to-top" id="bottom">'

                     +'  <a href="javascript:void(0);" data-currPage="1"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-load-more"><i class="icon icon-arrow-circle-down"></i><br class="visible-xs-block" />Weitere Nachrichten</button></a>'

                     + '</div>';
     
     var $ajax_button    = $("div.ajax-container-button:last");
     var $ajax_container = $("div.ajax-container-items:last");
     
     
     function mkLazy() {
         $("img.lazy").lazy({
              effect: "fadeIn",
              effectTime: 200,
              bind: "event",
              // css-Klasse "lazy" entfernen nach dem Laden
              afterLoad: function(element) {
                  element.removeClass("lazy");
              }
         });
     }
     
     
     
   $(document).ready(function () {
       $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
  
       if( history.state != null) {
         $ajax_container.html(history.state.ajax_content);
         $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
         mkLazy();
       };
     
       $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
         scroll(0,0);
       });
 
       $('.SiteHeaderSticky_close').hide();
   });
  if( history.state != null) {
     var more_news_currPage = history.state.more_news_currPage;
  } else {
      var more_news_currPage = 1;
  }
  var more_news_maxPerPage = 10;
     
  $( ".ajax-container-button" ).on( "click", function() {
      $( this ).html(loading_gif );
    
      $.ajax({
         url: "news/ajax",
         data: { 
             currPage : more_news_currPage, 
             maxperpage : more_news_maxPerPage
         },
         error: function(xhr){
             $ajax_container.append('Leider können derzeit keine weiteren News geladen werden.');
         }, 
         success: function(result){
             more_news_currPage ++;
             $ajax_container.hide().append(result).fadeIn(300);
             $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
             $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
             mkLazy();
             history.pushState( {ajax_content: $ajax_container.html() , more_news_currPage: more_news_currPage }, '', '#bottom');
             $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
               scroll(0,0);
             });
         }
       });

                     +'<img src="/img/ajax-loader.gif" />'; 
                     +'</div>';
     var mehr_lesen = '<div class="m-t-4 styling-to-top" id="bottom">'

                     +'  <a href="javascript:void(0);" data-currPage="1"><button class="btn btn-primary btn-load-more"><i class="icon icon-arrow-circle-down"></i><br class="visible-xs-block" />Weitere Nachrichten</button></a>'

                     + '</div>';
     
     var $ajax_button    = $("div.ajax-container-button:last");
     var $ajax_container = $("div.ajax-container-items:last");
     
     
     function mkLazy() {
         $("img.lazy").lazy({
              effect: "fadeIn",
              effectTime: 200,
              bind: "event",
              // css-Klasse "lazy" entfernen nach dem Laden
              afterLoad: function(element) {
                  element.removeClass("lazy");
              }
         });
     }
     
     
     
   $(document).ready(function () {
       $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
  
       if( history.state != null) {
         $ajax_container.html(history.state.ajax_content);
         $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
         mkLazy();
       };
     
       $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
         scroll(0,0);
       });
 
       $('.SiteHeaderSticky_close').hide();
   });
  if( history.state != null) {
     var more_news_currPage = history.state.more_news_currPage;
  } else {
      var more_news_currPage = 1;
  }
  var more_news_maxPerPage = 10;
     
  $( ".ajax-container-button" ).on( "click", function() {
      $( this ).html(loading_gif );
    
      $.ajax({
         url: "news/ajax",
         data: { 
             currPage : more_news_currPage, 
             maxperpage : more_news_maxPerPage
         },
         error: function(xhr){
             $ajax_container.append('Leider können derzeit keine weiteren News geladen werden.');
         }, 
         success: function(result){
             more_news_currPage ++;
             $ajax_container.hide().append(result).fadeIn(300);
             $ajax_button.html(mehr_lesen);
             $("div.ajax-container-items").css('padding-top', '20px');
             mkLazy();
             history.pushState( {ajax_content: $ajax_container.html() , more_news_currPage: more_news_currPage }, '', '#bottom');
             $("div.go-to-top button").on('click', function() {
               scroll(0,0);
             });
         }
       });

   });
